SELECT EQUIPCODE,ORDERCODE,EXAMCODE,EXAMCODESUB,EQUIPRESULT,RESULT,REFJUDGE    
  FROM PATRESULT                                                               
 WHERE EXAMDATE    = '2021-05-17'                                     
   AND SAVESEQ     = 5
   AND BARCODE     = '2105170047'                                      
   AND EXAMCODE    <> ''                                                       

Update RESULTOFNUM                                     
   Set RESULTINDATE   = to_char(sysdate,'yyyymmdd')    
     , RESULTINTIME   = to_char(sysdate,'HH24MI')      
     , RESULTINID     = '1004'         
     , RESULTFLAG     = '1'                            
     , TEXTRESULTVAL  = '6.07'              
     , NUMRESULTVAL = '6.07'            
 Where SPCMNO         = '2105170047'           
   And ORDERCODE      = 'LH001'             
   And RESULTITEMCODE = 'XH002001'            
   And RESULTFLAG < '3'                                

Update REGISTINFOS                         
   Set RESULTSTATE  = '1'                  
      ,RsvAcptState = '4'                  
 Where SPCMNO       = '2105170047' 
   AND ORDERCODE    = 'LH001'   
   AND CLAS         = 4                    
   AND RESULTSTATE < '4'                   

Update RESULTOFNUM                                     
   Set RESULTINDATE   = to_char(sysdate,'yyyymmdd')    
     , RESULTINTIME   = to_char(sysdate,'HH24MI')      
     , RESULTINID     = '1004'         
     , RESULTFLAG     = '1'                            
     , TEXTRESULTVAL  = '0.2'              
     , NUMRESULTVAL = '0.2'            
 Where SPCMNO         = '2105170047'           
   And ORDERCODE      = 'LH001'             
   And RESULTITEMCODE = 'XH002308'            
   And RESULTFLAG < '3'                                

Update REGISTINFOS                         
   Set RESULTSTATE  = '1'                  
      ,RsvAcptState = '4'                  
 Where SPCMNO       = '2105170047' 
   AND ORDERCODE    = 'LH001'   
   AND CLAS         = 4                    
   AND RESULTSTATE < '4'
